          </a>
         </i>
        </li>
        <li>
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/Grupos_Antiterroristas_de_Liberaci%C3%B3n" title="Grupos Antiterroristas de Liberacin">
           Grupos Antiterroristas de Liberacin
          </a>
         </i>
         (GAL)
        </li>
        <li>
         <i>
          <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Guerrilleros_de_Cristo_Rey" title="Guerrilleros de Cristo Rey">
           Guerrilleros de Cristo Rey
          </a>
         </i>
        </li>
       </ul>
      </li>
      <li>
       Minor Basque nationalist and radical left wing groups:
       <ul>
        <li>
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/Iparretarrak" title="Iparretarrak">
           Iparretarrak
          </a>
         </i>
        </li>
        <li>
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/Iraultza" title="Iraultza">
           Iraultza
          </a>
         </i>
        </li>
        <li>
         <i>
          <a href="/wiki/Comandos_Aut%C3%B3nomos_Anticapitalistas" title="Comandos Autnomos Anticapitalistas">
           Comandos Autnomos Anticapitalistas
          </a>
         </i>
        </li>
        <li>
         <i>
          <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Euskal_Zuzentasuna&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Euskal Zuzentasuna (page does not exist)">
           Euskal Zuzentasuna
          </a>
         </i>
        </li>
        <li>
         <i>
          <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Hordago&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Hordago (page does not exist)">
           Hordago
          </a>
         </i>
         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">
          <a href="#cite_note-149">
           <span>
            [
           </span>
           149
           <span>
            ]
           </span>
          </a>
         </sup>
        </li>
       </ul>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Extant">
       Extant
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=ETA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Extant">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Irrintzi_(group)" title="Irrintzi (group)">
         Irrintzi
        </a>
       </i>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="International_links">
       International links
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=ETA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: International links">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:192px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Divis_Street_Murals,_Belfast,_May_2011_(05).JPG">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="4272" data-file-width="2848" height="285" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/Divis_Street_Murals%2C_Belfast%2C_May_2011_%2805%29.JPG/190px-Divis_Street_Murals%2C_Belfast%2C_May_2011_%2805%29.JPG" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/Divis_Street_Murals%2C_Belfast%2C_May_2011_%2805%29.JPG/285px-Divis_Street_Murals%2C_Belfast%2C_May_2011_%2805%29.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/Divis_Street_Murals%2C_Belfast%2C_May_2011_%2805%29.JPG/380px-Divis_Street_Murals%2C_Belfast%2C_May_2011_%2805%29.JPG 2x" width="190"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Divis_Street_Murals,_Belfast,_May_2011_(05).JPG" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        A republican mural in
        <a href="/wiki/Belfast" title="Belfast">
         Belfast
        </a>
        showing solidarity with the Basque nationalism.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <ul>
      <li>
       ETA is known to have had 'fraternal' contacts with the
       <a href="/wiki/Provisional_Irish_Republican_Army" title="Provisional Irish Republican Army">
        Provisional Irish Republican Army
       </a>
       ; the two groups have both, at times, characterized their struggles as parallel. Links between the two groups go back to at least March 1974.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">
        <a href="#cite_note-150">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         150
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151">
        <a href="#cite_note-151">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         151
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       ETA purchased
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Strela_2" title="Strela 2">
        Strela 2
       </a>
       surface-to-air missiles from the IRA and in 2001 unsuccessfully attempted to shoot down a jet carrying the Spanish Prime Minister,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jose_Maria_Aznar" title="Jose Maria Aznar">
        Jose Maria Aznar
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">
        <a href="#cite_note-152">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         152
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       It has also had links with other militant left-wing movements in Europe and in other places throughout the world.
      </li>
      <li>
       In 1999 ETA commandos teamed up with the (now self-dissolved)
       <a href="/wiki/Breton_Revolutionary_Army" title="Breton Revolutionary Army">
        Breton Revolutionary Army
       </a>
       to steal
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Titadyne" title="Titadyne">
        explosives
       </a>
       from magazines in
       <a href="/wiki/Brittany" title="Brittany">
        Brittany
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       The Colombian government stated that there are contacts between ETA and the Colombian guerrillas
       <a href="/wiki/FARC" title="FARC">
        FARC
       </a>
       . The recent capture of FARC's leaders computers, and leaked email exchanges between both groups, show that ETA members received training from FARC. Apparently FARC asked for help from ETA in order to conduct future attacks in Spain,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-tehrantimes1_153-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-tehrantimes1-153">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         153
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-France_24_154-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-France_24-154">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         154
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PeopleDaily_155-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-PeopleDaily-155">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         155
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       but the Anncol news agency later denied it, clarifying that the Spanish capital Madrid had been confused with a city in northern Colombia also named Madrid.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-France_24_154-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-France_24-154">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         154
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       Following a judicial investigation, it was reported that FARC and ETA held meetings in Colombia, exchanging information about combat tactics and methods of activating explosives through mobile phones. The two organizations were said to have met at least three times. One of the meetings involved two ETA representatives and two FARC leaders, at a FARC camp, and lasted for a week in 2003. FARC also offered to hide ETA fugitives while requesting anti-air missiles, as well as asking for ETA to supply medical experts who could work at FARC prison camps for more than a year. In addition, and more controversially, FARC also asked ETA to stage attacks and kidnappings on its behalf in Europe.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156">
        <a href="#cite_note-156">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         156
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       Italian author and
       <a href="/wiki/Mafia" title="Mafia">
        mafia
       </a>
       specialist
       <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Saviano" title="Roberto Saviano">
        Roberto Saviano
       </a>
       points to a relationship of the group with the mafia. According to this view, ETA trafficks
       <a href="/wiki/Cocaine" title="Cocaine">
        cocaine
       </a>
       which it gets via its FARC contacts, then trades it with the mafia for guns.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157">
        <a href="#cite_note-157">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         157
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       Some ex-militants have received
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Political_asylum" title="Political asylum">
        political asylum
       </a>
       in Latin American countries, such as Mexico and
       <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">
        Venezuela
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       Several ex-militants were sent from France through
       <a href="/wiki/Panama" title="Panama">
        Panama
       </a>
       to reside in
       <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">
        Cuba
       </a>
       after an agreement of the Spanish government (under
       <a href="/wiki/Felipe_Gonz%C3%A1lez" title="Felipe Gonzlez">
        Felipe Gonzlez
       </a>
       ) with Cuba.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cuban_158-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Cuban-158">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         158
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
       The
       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_State" title="United States Department of State">
        United States Department of State
       </a>
       has no information on their activities on Cuban territory.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DoS_159-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-DoS-159">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         159
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="In_the_media">

      <span class="mw-editsection">

     </h2>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Films">
       Films
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=ETA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Films">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Documentary_films">
       Documentary films
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=ETA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Documentary films">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h4>
     <ul>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0291024/" rel="nofollow">
        <i>
         Asesinato en febrero
        </i>
       </a>
       at the
       <a href="/wiki/Internet_Movie_Database" title="Internet Movie Database">
        Internet Movie Database
       </a>
       , about the families of Basque politician
       <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Buesa" title="Fernando Buesa">
        Fernando Buesa
       </a>
       and his bodyguard, both killed by ETA.
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Basque_Ball" title="The Basque Ball">
         The Basque Ball: The Skin Against the Stone
        </a>
       </i>
       , (
       <i>
        La Pelota Vasca
       </i>
       , 2003) about the Basque conflict by filmmaker
       <a href="/wiki/Julio_Medem" title="Julio Medem">
        Julio Medem
       </a>
       : interviews about Basque nationalism and politics. Includes testimonials of ETA victims and relatives of ETA prisoners.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0442407/" rel="nofollow">
        <i>
         Perseguidos
        </i>
       </a>
       at the
       <a href="/wiki/Internet_Movie_Database" title="Internet Movie Database">
        Internet Movie Database
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Eterio_Ortega&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Eterio Ortega (page does not exist)">
        Eterio Ortega
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/El%C3%ADas_Querejeta" title="Elas Querejeta">
        Elas Querejeta
       </a>
       interview local councillors threatened by ETA.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0486499/" rel="nofollow">
        <i>
         Trece entre mil
        </i>
       </a>
       at the
       <a href="/wiki/Internet_Movie_Database" title="Internet Movie Database">
        Internet Movie Database
       </a>
       , the testimony of some of ETA's victims in the last 30 years by filmmaker
       <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=I%C3%B1aki_Arteta&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Iaki Arteta (page does not exist)">
        Iaki Arteta
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       48 horas: A movie about the kidnapping of Miguel Angel Blanco and his subsequent murder
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=ETA._Une_histoire_basque&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="ETA. Une histoire basque (page does not exist)">
         ETA. Une histoire basque
        </a>
       </i>
       , about the history of ETA
      </li>
      <li>
       In 2009 a video posted on YouTube subtitled in French shows an inside view of an ETA cell with their methods of action, notably, bomb making and ID card falsification. Also, there is footage of outdoor military training and of the Basque Warrior Day (Gudari Eguna)
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160">
        <a href="#cite_note-160">
         <span>
          [
         </span>
         160
         <span>
          ]
         </span>
        </a>
       </sup>
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.docsonline.tv/doc/749" rel="nofollow">
        Chronique Basque
       </a>
       About a Basque politician who is the target of an ETA death threat.
      </li>
     </ul>
     <h4>

      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">

       </i>

      </li>

         Operacin Ogro
        </a>
       </i>
       (Operation
       <a href="/wiki/Ogre" title="Ogre">
        Ogre
       </a>
       , 1979),
       <a href="/wiki/Gillo_Pontecorvo" title="Gillo Pontecorvo">

       </a>
       's film about the assassination of Luis Carrero Blanco.
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        El proceso de Burgos
       </i>
       ("The Burgos Trial", Imanol Uribe, 1979)
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0082424/" rel="nofollow">
        <i>
         Escape from Segovia (1981)
        </i>
       </a>
       at the
       <a href="/wiki/Internet_Movie_Database" title="Internet Movie Database">
        Internet Movie Database
       </a>

       <a href="/wiki/Segovia" title="Segovia">
        Segovia
       </a>
       prison.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0098131/" rel="nofollow">
        <i>
         Proceso a ETA
        </i>
       </a>
       at the
       <a href="/wiki/Internet_Movie_Database" title="Internet Movie Database">
        Internet Movie Database
       </a>
       ("The Trial of ETA", Manuel Maci, 1988)
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/Yoyes" title="Yoyes">
        Yoyes
       </a>
       , Mara Dolores Katarain, also known as Yoyes, tries to leave ETA and is killed by her former comarades.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a href="/wiki/The_Wolf_(film)" title="The Wolf (film)">
        El lobo
       </a>
       , based on the life of
       <a href="/wiki/Mikel_Lejarza" title="Mikel Lejarza">
        Mikel Lejarza
       </a>
       , who, prompted by the Spanish police, entered ETA to be a
       <a href="/wiki/Double_agent" title="Double agent">
        double agent
       </a>
       .
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt0498800/" rel="nofollow">
        <i>
         GAL
        </i>
       </a>
       at the
       <a href="/wiki/Internet_Movie_Database" title="Internet Movie Database">
        Internet Movie Database
       </a>
       , about the journalistic research leading to the uncovering of the state-supported GAL.
      </li>
      <li>
       <i>
        Tiro en la Cabeza
       </i>
       (2008) (A bullet in the head), about the life of an ETA member the day he will kill two Spanish Policemen in Capbreton, France.
      </li>
      <li>
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.imdb.com/title/tt1298818/" rel="nofollow">
        <i>
         Una Bala Para el Rey
        </i>
       </a>
       at the
       <a href="/wiki/Internet_Movie_Database" title="Internet Movie Database">
        Internet Movie Database
       </a>
       ("A Bullet for the King", March 2009) about ETA's failed plot to murder
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Juan_Carlos_I" title="Juan Carlos I">
        Juan CarlosI
       </a>
       during his holidays in
       <a href="/wiki/Majorca" title="Majorca">
        Majorca
       </a>
       in 1995.
      </li>
     </ul>

         <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AETA&amp;rft.atitle=Cincuenta+y+seis+etarras+han+muerto+en+enfrentamientos+con+las+fuerzas+de+seguridad&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.abc.es%2Fhemeroteca%2Fhistorico-15-09-2003%2Fabc%2FNacional%2Fcincuenta-y-seis-etarras-han-muerto-en-enfrentamientos-con-las-fuerzas-de-seguridad_207653.html&amp;rft.jtitle=ABC&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal">
          <span style="display:none;">
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </li>
       <li id="cite_note-publico-68">
        <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
         ^
         <a href="#cite_ref-publico_68-0">
          <sup>
           <i>
            <b>
             a
            </b>

          </sup>
         </a>
         <a href="#cite_ref-publico_68-1">
          <sup>
           <i>
            <b>
             b
            </b>
           </i>
          </sup>
         </a>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
         <a class="external text" href="http://www.publico.es/espana/037038/eta/comando/t4/torturas" rel="nofollow">
          ETA aleccion al 'comando' de la T-4 sobre cmo denunciar torturas  Pblico.es
         </a>
         . Publico.es. Retrieved on 30 January 2011.
        </span>
       </li>
       <li id="cite_note-AIUN2002-69">
        <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
         <b>
          <a href="#cite_ref-AIUN2002_69-0">
           ^
          </a>
         </b>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
         <a class="external text" href="http://web.amnesty.org/library/index/ENGEUR410122002" rel="nofollow">
          October 2002 AI Index: EUR 41/12/2002: SPAIN: A briefing for the United Nations Committee against Torture
         </a>
         :
         <i>
          Although convictions of torturers occur, these are rare.... examining judges and prosecutors may not always be displaying due diligence... trials involving torture complaints are often delayed for long periods. Where torture has been found to have occurred and torturers are convicted, awards of compensation by courts to torture victims are usually low and may take between seven and 19 years to be decided.
         </i>
        </span>
       </li>
       <li id="cite_note-AIUN2002Update-70">
        <span class="mw-cite-backlink">
         <b>
          <a href="#cite_ref-AIUN2002Update_70-0">
           ^
          </a>
         </b>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
         <a class="external text" href="http://web.amnesty.org/library/index/ENGEUR410142002" rel="nofollow">
          AI Index: EUR 41/014/2002: 1 November 2002: SPAIN: A Briefing for the UN Committee against Torture: Update
         </a>
         :
         <i>
          The Committee also expressed concern about: the length of judicial investigations into torture complaints, which could give rise to the granting of pardons to convicted torturers, or the failure to impose appropriate sentences, owing to the period of time that had elapsed since the crime was committed;
         </i>
        </span>

          </a>
         </b>
        </span>
        <span class="reference-text">
         <a class="external text" href="http://www.state.gov/s/ct/rls/crt/2005/64337.htm" rel="nofollow">
          Country Reports on Terrorism: Released by the Office of the Coordinator for Counterterrorism
         </a>
         (28 April 2006):
         <i>
          The Government of Cuba maintains close relationships with other state sponsors of terrorism such as
          <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">
           Iran
          </a>
          and
          <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">
           North Korea
          </a>
          , and has provided safe haven to members of
         </i>
         ETA
         <i>
          , FARC, and the
          <a href="/wiki/National_Liberation_Army_(Colombia)" title="National Liberation Army (Colombia)">
           ELN
          </a>
          .
         </i>
         There is no information concerning activities of these or other organizations on Cuban territory. Press reports indicate that fugitives from US justice and ETA members are living legally in Cuba, just like fugitives from Cuban justice live legally in the US. The United States says it is not aware of specific terrorist enclaves in the country.
        </span>
